namespace = ehof_travel

########################################################################################################
############################################## EHOF Travel #############################################
########################################################################################################

country_event = {
	id = ehof_travel.001
	title = "ehof_ehof"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_window"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		graphical_culture = root
		room = "ehof_room"
	}
	location = event_target:ehof_megastructure_system
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 } } text = "ehof_travel.001_01_desc" }
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } text = "ehof_travel.001_02_desc" }
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } text = "ehof_travel.001_03_desc" }
	desc = { trigger = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 4 } } text = "ehof_travel.001_04_desc" }

	trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy } }
	immediate = {
	    log = ui_1
		ehof_mega_system = yes
		set_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy
		remove_country_flag = ehof_alerted_recently
		#if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		OR = {
		#			has_country_flag = ehof_activating
		#			has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
		#		}
		#		NOT = { has_country_flag = ehof_destination_picked }
		#	}
		#	ehof_pre_flight = yes
		#}
	}

	###############################################################################################################
	# DESTINATIONS ################################################################################################
	###############################################################################################################
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_header"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ehof_activating
				has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			}
		}
		name = "ehof_header_01"
		hidden_effect = { remove_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy country_event = { id = ehof_travel.001 } }
	}

	# Wormhole Cohesive
	option = {
		name = "ehof_category_01"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ehof_activating
				has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 4 }
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 }
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 }
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 }
			}
		}
		allow = {
			if = {		limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p3 } }
			else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @ehof_target_p2 } }
			else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @ehof_target_p1 } }
		}
		if = {		limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p3 } }
		else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } add_resource = { energy = @ehof_target_neg_p2 } }
		else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 } } add_resource = { energy = @ehof_target_neg_p1 } }
		hidden_effect = { ehof_dest_01 = yes }
	}

	# Random
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ehof_activating
				has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			}
			check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value <= 4 }
		}
		allow = {
			if = {		limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 4 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 } }
			else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p3 } }
			else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @ehof_target_p2 } }
			else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @ehof_target_p1 } }
		}
		if = {		limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 4 } } add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p4 } }
		else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p3 } }
		else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } add_resource = { energy = @ehof_target_neg_p2 } }
		else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 1 } } add_resource = { energy = @ehof_target_neg_p1 } }
		name = "ehof_category_00"
		hidden_effect = { ehof_pre_flight = yes ehof_dest_02 = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = "ehof_category_06"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			any_system = {
				ehof_travel_conditions = yes
				cohesive_system = no
				compound_cluster = no
				annihilator_system = no
				urmazin_system = no
				everchanging_system = no
				is_binary = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ehof_activating
				has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 4 }
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 }
			}
		}
		allow = {
			if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p3 } }
		}
		if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p3 } }
		hidden_effect = { ehof_pre_flight = yes ehof_dest_03 = yes }
	}

	option = {

		trigger = {
			any_system = {
				ehof_travel_conditions = yes
				cohesive_system = no
				compound_cluster = no
				annihilator_system = no
				urmazin_system = no
				everchanging_system = no
				is_star_class_sc_m_super = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ehof_activating
				has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 4 }
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 }
				check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 }
			}
		}
		allow = {
			if = {		limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p3 } }
			else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = energy value >= @ehof_target_p2 } }
		}
		if = {		limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 3 } } add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p3 } }
		else_if = {	limit = { check_variable = { which = ehof_phase value = 2 } } add_resource = { energy = @ehof_target_neg_p2 } }
		hidden_effect = { ehof_pre_flight = yes ehof_dest_27 = yes }
	}

# Pick a specific star
country_event = {
	id = ehof_travel.002
	title = "ehof_ehof"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_window"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		graphical_culture = root
		room = "ehof_room"
	}
	location = event_target:ehof_megastructure_system
	desc = "ehof_travel.001_04_desc"

	immediate = {
	    log = ui_2
		ehof_mega_system = yes
		giga_event_target_list_clear = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_d }
			every_system = {
				limit = {
					is_star_class_sc_d = yes
					cohesive_system = no
					compound_cluster = no

	# Annihilator System
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_cohesive }
			has_global_flag = annihilator_system_spawned
		}
		allow = { resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 } }
		name = "ehof_system_unknown"
		hidden_effect = {
		    ehof_pre_flight = yes
			random_system = {
				limit = { annihilator_system = yes }
				open_wormhole = yes
			}
		}
	}

	# Trader Hub
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_cohesive }
			has_global_flag = ehof_traders_spawned
		}
		allow = { resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 } }
		name = "ehof_system_traders"
		hidden_effect = { ehof_pre_flight = yes event_target:urmazin_capital = { open_wormhole = yes } }
	}

	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_blank"
		name = "ehof_header_blank"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_cohesive
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = annihilator_system_spawned
				has_global_flag = ehof_traders_spawned
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ehof_travel.002 } }
	}

	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_header"
		trigger = {
			any_system = {
				ehof_travel_conditions = yes
				OR = {
					root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_cohesive }
					AND = { root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_d }				is_star_class_sc_d = yes }
					AND = { root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_g }				is_star_class_sc_g = yes NOT = { has_star_flag = flusion_system } }

					AND = { root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_s_giant }		is_star_class_sc_c_giant = yes }
					AND = { root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_ae }			is_star_class_sc_ae = yes }
					AND = { root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_binary }			is_binary = yes }
					AND = { root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_trinary }			is_trinary = yes }
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_black_hole }
						OR = {
							is_star_class = sc_black_hole
							is_star_class = sc_birch
							is_star_class = sc_ehof_black_hole
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_nova_1 }
						OR = {
							is_star_class_sc_nova_1 = yes
							is_star_class_sc_nova_2 = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_quasar }
						OR = {
							is_star_class = sc_quasar
							is_star_class_sc_microquasar_1 = yes
							is_star_class_sc_microquasar_2 = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_brown }
						OR = {
							is_star_class_sc_t = yes
							is_star_class_sc_l = yes
							is_star_class_sc_y = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_lbv_blue }
						OR = {
							is_star_class_sc_lbv_blue = yes
							is_star_class_sc_lbv_green = yes
							is_star_class_sc_lbv_red = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_p_purple }
						OR = {
							is_star_class_sc_p_purple = yes
							is_star_class_sc_p_red = yes
							is_star_class_sc_p_green = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_tt_red }
						OR = {
							is_star_class_sc_tt_orange = yes
							is_star_class_sc_tt_red = yes
							is_star_class_sc_tt_white = yes
						}
					}
					AND = {
						root = { has_country_flag = giga_ehof_target_sc_w_azure }
						OR = {
							is_star_class_sc_w_azure = yes
							is_star_class_sc_w_red = yes
							is_star_class_sc_w_green = yes
							is_star_class_sc_w_purple = yes
						}
					}
				}
				empire_has_visited = no
				cohesive_system = no
				compound_cluster = no
				annihilator_system = no
				urmazin_system = no
				everchanging_system = no
			}
		}

# Create a specific star
country_event = {
	id = ehof_travel.003
	title = "ehof_ehof"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_window"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		graphical_culture = root
		room = "ehof_room"
	}
	location = event_target:ehof_megastructure_system
	desc = "ehof_travel.001_04_desc"

	immediate = { log = ui_3 ehof_mega_system = yes }

	# Spawn a birch system
	option = {
		name = "ehof_sm_blackhole"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_small"
		trigger = {
			has_ascension_perk = ap_vast_expanses
			NOT = { any_system = { is_star_class = sc_birch } }
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = ehof_sr_negative_mass value >= 15000 }
		}
		add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p4 }
		add_resource = { ehof_sr_negative_mass = -15000 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_birch
			#country_event = { id = ehof_systems.000 }
			#remove_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_birch
			#last_created_system = { open_wormhole = yes }
            set_country_flag = should_spawn_covesive_@root

            ehof_pre_flight = yes
		}
	}

	# Spawn a QSO system
	option = {
		name = "ehof_sm_quasar"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_small"
		trigger = {
			has_ascension_perk = ap_qso
			NOT = { any_system = { is_star_class = sc_quasar } }
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = ehof_sr_negative_mass value >= 15000 }
		}
		add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p4 }
		add_resource = { ehof_sr_negative_mass = -15000 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_quasar
			#country_event = { id = ehof_systems.000 }
			#remove_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_quasar
			#last_created_system = { open_wormhole = yes }
            set_country_flag = should_spawn_covesive_@root

            ehof_pre_flight = yes
		}
	}

	# Random
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 }
		}
		add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p4 }
		name = "ehof_category_00"
		hidden_effect = {
		    log = random_cohe
			#country_event = { id = ehof_systems.000 }
			#last_created_system = { open_wormhole = yes }
			set_country_flag = should_spawn_covesive_@root

			ehof_pre_flight = yes
		}
	}

	#############################
	# Dwarves ###################
	#############################
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_miniheader"
		name = "ehof_category_02"
		hidden_effect = { remove_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy country_event = { id = ehof_travel.003 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "sc_f"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_small"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = ehof_sr_negative_mass value >= @ehof_create_p4 }
		}
		add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p4 }
		add_resource = { ehof_sr_negative_mass = @ehof_create_neg_p4 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_f
			#country_event = { id = ehof_systems.000 }

		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_small"
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = sr_dark_matter value >= @ehof_target_p4 }
			resource_stockpile_compare = { resource = ehof_sr_negative_mass value >= @ehof_create_p4 }
		}
		add_resource = { sr_dark_matter = @ehof_target_neg_p4 }
		add_resource = { ehof_sr_negative_mass = @ehof_create_neg_p4 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_pulsar
			#country_event = { id = ehof_systems.000 }
			#remove_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_pulsar
			#last_created_system = { open_wormhole = yes }
			set_country_flag = should_spawn_covesive_@root

			ehof_pre_flight = yes
		}
	}
